    $(document).ready(function () {

        $('#rootContainer').css('margin-top', thirdLevelHeight);

<script type="text/javascript">

    vw = window.innerWidth;
    $(document).ready(function () {

        //Highlight first menu option as default -- 

        var _firstLi = $('.right').children('ul').children('li:nth-child(2)')
        var take = $(_firstLi).children('ul').html();
        $(this).children('ul').focus();
        var put = $('.left ul');
        put.html(take);

        if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 70) {
            $("nav").addClass("nav-scrolled");
        }

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            var scroll = $(window).scrollTop();
            if (scroll >= 70) {
                if ($('.sidenav').hasClass('sidenav-open') && vw < 769) {
                    $("nav").removeClass("nav-scrolled");
                } else {
                    $("nav").addClass("nav-scrolled");
                }
            } else {
                $("nav").removeClass("nav-scrolled");
            }
        });

        $('.right').scroll(function () {
            var rightScroll = $('.right').scrollTop();
            if (rightScroll >= 70) {
                $('.close-outer').show();
                $("nav").addClass("nav-scrolled-light");
            } else {
                $("nav").removeClass("nav-scrolled-light");
                $('.close-outer').fadeOut();
            }
        });

        if (vw > 769) {
            $('.right .outer').mouseover(function () {
                var take = $(this).children('ul').html();
                $(this).children('ul').focus();
                if (take != undefined) {
                    var put = $('.left ul');
                    put.html(take);
                } else {
                    $('.left ul').html('<li> nothing here/li>');
                }
            });
        } else {

            $('.right .outer').click(function () {
                if ($(this).hasClass('li-open')) {
                    $(this).removeClass('li-open');
                } else {
                    $('.right .outer').removeClass('li-open');
                    $(this).addClass('li-open');
                }
            });
            $('.right .inner').click(function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
            });
        }

        function menuClicked(e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
            $('.sidenav').toggleClass('sidenav-open');
            $('.menu').toggleClass('menuToClose');
            $('.search-open').removeClass('search-open');
            $('.news-bar').fadeToggle();

            if (vw < 769) {
                $("nav").removeClass("nav-scrolled");
            }
            if ($('section').scrollTop() >= 70 && !$('.sidenav').hasClass('sidenav-open')) {
                $("nav").addClass("nav-scrolled");
            }
            if ($('.right').scrollTop() >= 70) {
                $(".close-outer").show();
                $("nav").addClass("nav-scrolled-light");
            } else {
                $(".close-outer").hide();
                $("nav").removeClass("nav-scrolled-light");
            }
        }

        $('.menubtn').click(function (e) {
            menuClicked(e);
        });

        $('.search span').click(function (e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
            $('.search-open').removeClass('search-open');
            $('.close-menu').css('opacity', '1');
        });

        $('.sidenav').click(function (e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
        });

        $('.close-menu').click(function () {
            $('.sidenav').removeClass('sidenav-open');
            $('.menu').removeClass('menuToClose');
            $("nav").removeClass("nav-scrolled-light");
        });

        $('.close-outer').click(function () {
            $(this).hide();
            $("nav").removeClass("nav-scrolled-light");
            if ($(window).scrollTop() > 70) {
                $("nav").addClass("nav-scrolled");
            }
        });

        $('html').click(function (e) {
            $('.sidenav').removeClass('sidenav-open');
            $('.menu').removeClass('menuToClose');
            $('.search-open').removeClass('search-open');

            if ($(window).scrollTop() >= 70) {
                $("nav").addClass("nav-scrolled");
            }
        });

        $('.search').click(function (e) {
            e.stopPropagation();
            $(this).parents('ul').addClass('search-open');
            $('.close-menu').css('opacity', '0');
        });

        $('.inner li').each(function () {
            var x = $(this).children('a').text();
            if (x === '') {
                $(this).remove();
            }
        });

        $(document).on('keypress', function (e) {
            if (e.which == 13 && $(".menubtn").is(":focus")) {
                menuClicked(e);
            }
        });

    });

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    //Test Token: 12548092454.1677ed0.d5d5032fc08848db92a7eb1d0b452b37
    //IAF-site token: 343574815.1677ed0.abd61dac20b24e518cd10164bb01f763
    var token = '343574815.1677ed0.abd61dac20b24e518cd10164bb01f763', // learn how to obtain it below

        //test user id: 12548092454
        //iaf-site user id: 343574815
        userid = 343574815, // User ID - get it in source HTML of your Instagram profile or look at the next example :)
        num_photos = 3; // how much photos do you want to get

    $.ajax({
        url: 'https://api.instagram.com/v1/users/' + userid + '/media/recent', // or /users/self/media/recent for Sandbox
        dataType: 'jsonp',
        type: 'GET',
        data: { access_token: token, count: num_photos },
        success: function (data) {           
            for (x in data.data) {           
                $('.insta-feed').prepend(
                    '<a class="img-wrap" href="'+data.data[x].link +'" target="_blank" style="background-image:url('+data.data[x].images.low_resolution.url +')" > </a>');             
            }
        },
        error: function (data) {            
        }
    });
</script>
